if (!is_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml') != '7e01767f8dd0f2bb4ff93bd23364bbd8836f371f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml') !== '7e01767f8dd0f2bb4ff93bd23364bbd8836f371f') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml') !== '8f840afa5995416f6eee329dce0a7df0d9df1927') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml') !== '7e01767f8dd0f2bb4ff93bd23364bbd8836f371f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/inspectionProfiles/Project_Default.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('.idea/workspace.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: .idea/workspace.xml');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('.idea/workspace.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .idea/workspace.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') != '1fca7e3f9dcb2fb951f91fb51a8f54d08540b765') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .idea/workspace.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/workspace.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/workspace.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== '1fca7e3f9dcb2fb951f91fb51a8f54d08540b765') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== '8d957029a63509c1a5d495f73b66fa4b1358f813') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/workspace.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/workspace.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/workspace.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/workspace.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/workspace.xml') !== '1fca7e3f9dcb2fb951f91fb51a8f54d08540b765') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/workspace.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'bd91dc180a9c75e7d5bdc130059c375e996b2f5c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'bd91dc180a9c75e7d5bdc130059c375e996b2f5c') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '2bcf261165ef2478c323413951c1777654021d40') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'bd91dc180a9c75e7d5bdc130059c375e996b2f5c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') != 'ca82ee7d7bd8604811e3cc9ac57d6a3648adfc92') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') !== 'ca82ee7d7bd8604811e3cc9ac57d6a3648adfc92') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') !== 'e44b3f2a38376ffe00fec1c3523810a4090c649f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') !== 'ca82ee7d7bd8604811e3cc9ac57d6a3648adfc92') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.min.css.php');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.css.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') != '59803125b9939ad73cc33d9e5565ae7372cc8c67') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.css.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.css.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '59803125b9939ad73cc33d9e5565ae7372cc8c67') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== 'cb5131b9ed92f8e269e391f96ca9e8299755c8d9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.css.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.css.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.css.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.css.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '59803125b9939ad73cc33d9e5565ae7372cc8c67') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
		}
	}
}
